{"nick":"Sorella","message":"Rou: Rust is a functional language with linear types and CSP-based concurrency (the same as Go). It means you don't need a GC, because the compiler can enforce safe usage of *every* resource from the type system alone (so every resource life cycle is fixed at compile time, from the types). It has a focus on safety (it's impossible to do unsafe things in","date":"2015-09-16T13:47:46.590Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"Sorella","message":"Rust, outside of unsafe blocks).
